 Frequent use of banks' atms can be costly from November
 rigerv bank ne chah mahanagaron main atm kaa free istemaal simit karne kaa faisla kiya he
 Whether you withdraw money or take only account information, you will have to pay a fee of Rs 20 for usage beyond the fixed number
 desh ke chah mahanagaron main kisi duusare bank ke ‚Äòautomated tailor mashin- atm‚Äô kaa istemaal maheene main keval teen baar free hoga, jabaki apane hi bank ke atm se keval paanch baar hi free lenden ho sakegaa
 For this, customers will have to pay a fee of Rs 20 each time
 dilli, mumbai, chennai, bengalooru, kolkata or hyderabad main november se atm se rupee nikaalane kii yah nai vyavastha lagu hogi
 The memorandum was sent to the Reserve Bank of India by the Banks Association of India (IBA)
 rigerv bank kii jari adhisuchana main kaha gaya he, ‚Äòbachat khaataa dharakon ko duusare bainkon ke atm kaa istemaal karne par anivaary rup se free lenden kii sankhya maujuuda paanch se ghataakar teen pratimah kar di gai he
 This includes both financial and non-financial transactions
 yah vyavastha desh ke chah mahanagaron sthit atm par lagu hogi
 'use of your own bank ATM will be free five times every month
 chaahe paisa nikaalen yaa keval khate kii jaankaree len, maheene main paanch baar apane bank ke atm kaa istemaal free hoga
 Banks will be allowed to charge Rs 20 for using more atms than the prescribed number
 rigerv bank ne haalanki yah bhi spasht kiya he ki nai vyavastha chote, no-frill or basic bachat khaataa dharakon ke khaaton par lagu nahin hogi
 Apart from the six metros of the country, the new system will not be applicable in other cities

 So know 10 tips that will solve every problem related to your hair this season
 
 
 garmiyon main baalo kii dekhbhaal karne ke ye 5 tips jarur aajamaayen
 
 
 - On the weekend, definitely apply oil to your hair and keep it parting
 isse baalo ko poshan milegaa
 - When you reach home in the evening, do comb hair, then tie hair
 - baalo par hair dryer aadi kaa prayog naa karen, isse bal or ruukhe ho jate hai or tuutane lagate hai
 - When you exit, cover the head with a cloth
 bahut kam logon ko pataa hoga ki dhoop kaa asar baalo par bhi padataa he
 Do you know the right way to shampoo? - Massage with coconut, olive oil before washing hair
 pratidin bal naa dhoen, isse scalp main maujuud prakritik tel nikal sakate hai, jisase bal rukhe ho sakate hai or baar-baar bal dhone kii jarurat mahasoos ho sakati he
 - Use Ammonia Free Hair Colors to color your hair
 ye inke dushprabhav se bachaate hai or baalo ko poshan dete hai
 If hair is falling, take care not to be fooled - Whenever you go to the pool etc
, you must come back and wash your hair
 - kanghee karte hue hair brush kii bajaay chaude daanton vaali kanghee kaa istemaal karen
 - Do not comb wet hair
 isse bal tuutate hai
 - With increasing temperature, replace hair serum with hair oil
 yah kam chipchipa hota he

 is sambandh main supreme court baar association ke upaadhyaksh or senior edwocket jitendra mohan sharma kaa kahana he ki 18 saal kii umr puri kar chuki har ladki or 21 saal kii umr puri kar chuke har ladke ko apni marji se shaadi karne kaa moulik adhikaar he
 The Supreme Court, the country's largest court, has said many times in its judgment that the right to marry falls under the right to life found in Article 21 of the Indian Constitution
 is adhikaar ko koi nahin chin saktaa he
 They say that if the girl has attained the age of 18 years and the boy has attained the age of 21 years, then they can marry
 unki shaadi main jati, dharm, kshetra or bhashaa jaisi chijen baadha nahin banati hai

 yahi baat ladke ke upar bhi lagu hoti he
 Jitendra Mohan Sharma, Senior Advocate of the Supreme Court said that if the boy is 21 years of age, then he can marry a citizen of any caste, religion or any other country

 The condition for marriage is only that the mental state of the boy or girl should be corrected, so that they can give their consent for marriage
 aapako bataa den ki shaadi ke liye hindu marij act, special marij act, indian chrishchiyan marij act or fahrren marij act samet kai act banaae gaye hai

 iske liye kisi se ijaajat kii jarurat nahin hoti he
